## Opcodes

```
  0: 0x2A0C [0x42] SET_CLI_EVENT_CANCEL_DATA()
  1: 0x2A0D [0x45] LOAD_SCHEDULED_TASK(work_offset1=200*, entity1=LocalPlayer, entity2=LocalPlayer, scheduler_id="fdo1", work_offset2=0*)

  4: 0x2A2F [0x38] SET_CLIENT_EVENT_MODE(mode=19*)

  6: 0x2A37 [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[3] = Work_Zone[3]
```
